    var NW = {
        waitForFunctionAvailability: function (functionName, callback, interval = 1000, maxAttempts = 10) {
            let attempts = 0;

            const checkFunction = setInterval(() => {
                // Function found, clear interval and call the function.
                if (typeof window[functionName] === 'function') {
                    console.log('function found');
                    clearInterval(checkFunction);
                    callback();
                } else if (attempts >= maxAttempts) {
                    // Function not found after max attempts, clear the interval.
                    console.log('function not found');
                    clearInterval(checkFunction);
                }

                attempts++;
            }, interval);
        },
        // Cookies
        getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            var name = cookieName + "=";
            var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
            var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
            for(var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                var c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0) === ' ') {
                    c = c.substring(1);
                }
                if (c.indexOf(name) === 0) {
                    return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                }
            }
            return "";
        },
        // setCookie('myCookie', myParam, 7); // Ersetze 'myCookie' mit dem Namen deines Cookies und 7 mit der Anzahl der Tage, bis der Cookie abläuft
        setCookie(name, value, daysToExpire) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + (daysToExpire * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
            var expires = "expires=" + date.toUTCString();
            document.cookie = name + "=" + value + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
        },
        removeCookie(name) {
            document.cookie = name + "=;expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT;path=/";
        }
    };

        function engagentlyCommentCount(elementSelector = '.egyCounter') {
        const EGY_COMMUNITY_ID = "nw9Ljb87d2";
        const counters = document.querySelectorAll(`${elementSelector}`);
        if (counters.length > 0) {
            const discussionIds = Array.from(counters).map((counter) =>
                counter.getAttribute("data-egy-dsc")
            );
            const apiBatchUrl = `https://ct${EGY_COMMUNITY_ID}.engagently.com/counts/commentaries/${EGY_COMMUNITY_ID}/batch`;


            fetch(apiBatchUrl, {
                method: "POST",
                headers: {
                    "Content-Type": "application/json",
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({discussion_ids: discussionIds}),
            })
                .then((response) => response.json())
                .then((data) => {
                    for (const counter of counters) {
                        const discussionId = counter.getAttribute("data-egy-dsc");
                        var article_comments_parent = counter.closest(".article-comments");
                        const count = data?.[discussionId];
                        if (typeof count !== "number" || count == 0) {
                            article_comments_parent.classList.add('nw-hidden');
                            continue;
                        } else if (count > 0) {
                            counter.innerHTML = count;
                            article_comments_parent.classList.remove('nw-hidden');
                        }
                        if (count > 99) {
                            counter.innerHTML = '99+';
                            article_comments_parent.classList.remove("nw-w-6");
                            article_comments_parent.classList.add("nw-w-9");
                        }

                    }
                })
                .catch((error) => console.error("Error loading comment count:", error));
        }

    }

    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        engagentlyCommentCount();
    });
    </script>

<script>

    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
        var loginInitiated = false;
        if (!loginInitiated) {
            var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
            xhr.open('GET', '/_em_cms/globals/modul.php?modul=modul_login_box', true);
            xhr.setRequestHeader('Cache-Control', 'no-cache');
            xhr.responseType = "document";
            xhr.onload = function () {
                if (xhr.status >= 200 && xhr.status < 300) {
                    //var html = xhr.response.documentElement.innerHTML;

                    var responseDoc = xhr.response;
                    var html = responseDoc.documentElement.innerHTML;
                    var container = document.createElement('div');
                    container.innerHTML = html;
                    document.getElementById("em_login_head").insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', container.innerHTML);

                    // Extract and execute scripts
                    var scripts = container.getElementsByTagName('script');
                    for (var i = 0; i < scripts.length; i++) {
                        var script = document.createElement('script');
                        if (scripts[i].src) {
                            // If the script has a src attribute, dynamically create a script element
                            script.src = scripts[i].src;
                        } else {
                            // If the script contains inline code, set its text content
                            script.textContent = scripts[i].textContent;
                        }
                        document.head.appendChild(script);
                    }

                    if (window.location.href.indexOf("#open-login") !== -1) {
                        document.getElementById('nw-loginbox').classList.remove("nw-hidden");
                        document.getElementById('nw-loginbox').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
                    }
                    document.getElementById('nw-loginbox').style.zIndex = 9999999999;

                    var loginboxNavbarDestination = document.getElementById("#loginbox-navbar-destination");
                    var loginboxNavbar = document.getElementById("#loginbox-navbar");
                    if (loginboxNavbarDestination && loginboxNavbar) {
                        loginboxNavbarDestination.parentNode.replaceChild(loginboxNavbar, loginboxNavbarDestination);
                    }

                    var loginErrorSource = document.getElementById("em_login_error_source");
                    var loginErrorDestination = document.getElementById("em_login_error_destination");
                    if (loginErrorSource && loginErrorDestination) {
                        loginErrorDestination.innerHTML = loginErrorSource.innerHTML;
                        toggleLoginBox(false);
                    }

                    var xsLogin = document.getElementById("xs-login");
                    var xsLoginSource = document.getElementById("xs-login-source");
                    if (xsLogin && xsLoginSource) {
                        xsLogin.parentNode.replaceChild(xsLoginSource, xsLogin);
                    }

                    if (loginErrorSource) {
                        document.getElementById('nw-loginbox').classList.remove('nw-hidden') ;
                        document.getElementById('background-popup').classList.remove('nw-hidden');
                    }
                }
            };
            xhr.send();
            loginInitiated = true;
        }
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
        function triggerCacheLog(userstatus_upscore, sso_id, sso_hash, user_token, pw_cookie, plus_article) {
        console.log('cache-log: ' + document.getElementsByClassName('nw-overlay').length + ':' + userstatus_upscore);
        if (document.getElementsByClassName('nw-overlay').length === 1 && userstatus_upscore === 2 ) {
            var url = '/_apps/nw/test/sub-paywall-log.php';
            var data = { sso_id: sso_id, sso_hash: sso_hash, user_token: user_token, pw_cookie: pw_cookie, userstatus: userstatus_upscore, url: document.URL, useragent: window.navigator.userAgent, time: new Date};
            postAjax(url, data, function(data){ console.log(data); });
        }
        if (plus_article && document.getElementsByClassName('nw-overlay').length === 0 && userstatus_upscore < 2 ) {
            var url = '/_apps/nw/test/noabo-plusread-log.php';
            var data = { sso_id: sso_id, sso_hash: sso_hash, user_token: user_token, pw_cookie: pw_cookie, userstatus: userstatus_upscore, url: document.URL, useragent: window.navigator.userAgent, time: new Date};
            postAjax(url, data, function(data){ console.log(data); });
        }

    }

    function postAjax(url, data, success) {
        var params = typeof data == 'string' ? data : Object.keys(data).map(
            function(k){ return encodeURIComponent(k) + '=' + encodeURIComponent(data[k]) }
        ).join('&');

        var xhr = window.XMLHttpRequest ? new XMLHttpRequest() : new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
        xhr.open('POST', url);
        xhr.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (xhr.readyState>3 && xhr.status==200) { success(xhr.responseText); }
        };
        xhr.setRequestHeader('X-Requested-With', 'XMLHttpRequest');
        xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded');
        xhr.send(params);
        return xhr;
    }
</script>

<script>
    var audio = document.getElementById('summary_audio');
    function toggleContent() {
        var hiddenSection = document.getElementById('hiddenSection');
        var mehrSection = document.getElementById('mehrSection');
        var headerSection = document.getElementById('headerSection');
        var audioSection = document.getElementById('audioSection');
        if (hiddenSection.classList.contains('hiddensection')) {
            hiddenSection.classList.toggle('hiddensection');
            hiddenSection.classList.toggle('showSection');
            mehrSection.classList.toggle('nw-hidden');
            headerSection.classList.toggle('nw-hidden');
            audioSection.classList.toggle('nw-hidden');
            audioSection.classList.toggle('nw-block', !hiddenSection.classList.contains('hiddenSection'));
        } else {
            hiddenSection.classList.toggle('showSection');
            hiddenSection.classList.toggle('hiddensection');
            mehrSection.classList.toggle('nw-hidden');
            headerSection.classList.toggle('nw-hidden');
            audioSection.classList.toggle('nw-hidden');
            audioSection.classList.toggle('nw-block', !hiddenSection.classList.contains('hiddenSection'));
            audio.pause();
        }
    }
    document.getElementById('playButton').addEventListener('click', function() {
        audio.play();
    });

</script>

    <script>
        var user_token = '';
        var is_paid_user = '';
        // var is_paid_user = 0;
        function expand(module_id) {
            if(user_token == ''){
                return showModalBox('reg-modal');
            }else{
                if(!is_paid_user && !manageAudioSummaryAccess(module_id)){
                    return showModalBox('abo-modal');
                }
            }
            document.getElementById('collapsed_'+module_id).classList.add('nw-hidden');
            document.getElementById('expanded_'+module_id).classList.remove('nw-hidden');
            document.getElementById('play_button_'+module_id).classList.add('nw-hidden');
        }
        function collapse(module_id) {
            let audio_ = document.getElementById('summary_audio_'+module_id);
            audio_.pause();
            document.getElementById('collapsed_'+module_id).classList.remove('nw-hidden');
            document.getElementById('expanded_'+module_id).classList.add('nw-hidden');
            document.getElementById('play_button_'+module_id).classList.remove('nw-hidden');
            document.getElementById('play_button_'+module_id).scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
        }
        function playAudio(module_id) {
            console.log('playAudio');
            expand(module_id);
            if(user_token == ''){
                return '';
            }else if(!is_paid_user){
                let accessCount = localStorage.getItem('audioSummaryAccessCount_' + module_id);
                if (accessCount != null && parseInt(accessCount, 10) >= 5) {
                    return '';
                }
            }
            let audio_ = document.getElementById('summary_audio_'+module_id);
            // audio_.playbackRate = 1.25;
            audio_.play().catch(error => {
                console.error("Playback failed because:", error);
            });
        }
    //     modal boxes
        function showModalBox(id = 'abo-modal') {
            modal = document.getElementById(id);
            modal.classList.remove('nw-hidden');

            // ESC-Taste schließen
            // document.addEventListener('keydown', escListener);

            // Klick außerhalb des Inhalts schließt Modal
            // // modal.addEventListener('click', outsideClickListener());
            // modal.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
            //     outsideClickListener(event, modal);
            // });
        }

        function closeModal(id = 'abo-modal') {
            modal = document.getElementById(id);
            modal.classList.add('nw-hidden');
            document.removeEventListener('keydown', escListener);
            modal.removeEventListener('click', outsideClickListener);
        }
        function manageAudioSummaryAccess(module_id) {

            const accessCountKey = 'audioSummaryAccessCount_' + module_id; // Use module_id to differentiate access counts
            // const accessCountKey = 'audioSummaryAccessCount';
            let accessCount = localStorage.getItem(accessCountKey);

            // Initialize the count if it doesn't exist
            if (accessCount === null) {
                accessCount = 0;
            } else {
                accessCount = parseInt(accessCount, 10);
            }
            console.log('Current access count for module ' + module_id + ': ' + accessCount);
            if (accessCount < 5) {
                // Allow access and increment the count
                localStorage.setItem(accessCountKey, accessCount + 1);
                return true; // Access granted
            }
            // else if (accessCount === 4) {
            //     // Allow access this time and then show the widget for the next time
            //     if (audioSummaryElement) {
            //         audioSummaryElement.style.display = 'block'; // Or however you display the content
            //     }
            //     if (subscriptionWidget) {
            //         subscriptionWidget.style.display = 'none'; // Ensure the widget is hidden

<script>
    const pinpollWrappers = document.querySelectorAll('.pinpoll-wrapper');

    const pinpollObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        entries.forEach((entry) => {
            if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                const pinpollElement = entry.target.querySelector('[data-pinpoll-id]');
                const spinner = entry.target.querySelector('.loading-spinner');

                // Check if the poll is already loaded hide the spinner
                if (pinpollElement) {
                    pinpollElement.dataset.pollLoaded = 'true';
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        spinner.classList.add('nw-hidden');
                    }, 1000);

                    const wrapper = entry.target;

                    // MutationObserver for the iframe and if exist add title attribute
                    const iframeObserver = new MutationObserver((iframeMutationsList, iframeObserver) => {
                        const iframe = wrapper.querySelector('iframe');
                        if (iframe) {
                            iframe.title = 'Umfrage';
                            iframeObserver.disconnect();
                        }
                    });

                    // Existinf mutationObserver for the iframe and if exist add title attribute
                    const existingIframe = wrapper.querySelector('iframe');
                    if (existingIframe) {
                        existingIframe.title = 'Umfrage';
                        iframeObserver.disconnect();
                    } else {
                        iframeObserver.observe(wrapper, { childList: true, subtree: true });
                    }
                }
                pinpollObserver.unobserve(entry.target);
            }
        });
    });

    pinpollWrappers.forEach((wrapper) => {
        pinpollObserver.observe(wrapper);
    });
</script><!--This is a col-md-8 end.--></div><div class="content-right-col col-md-4">

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        // Store the base URL in a variable for use in the AJAX requests
        var baseUrl = window.location.href;
        $('input[id^="referrer_url"]').val(baseUrl);
        $(document).on('submit', '.nl-anmeldung-form', function (event) {
            event.preventDefault();


            var frm = $(this);
            var isFormValid = true;

            var nl_id = frm.find('input[name="nl_id"], select[name="nl_id"]').val();
            if (!nl_id) {
                frm.find('.error-message-nl_id').show();
                isFormValid = false;
            } else {
                frm.find('.error-message-nl_id').hide();
            }

            var email = frm.find('input[type="email"]').val();
            var emailRegex = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
            if (!email || !emailRegex.test(email)) {
                frm.find('.error-message-mail').show();
                isFormValid = false;
            } else {
                frm.find('.error-message-mail').hide();
            }

            if (!isFormValid) {
                event.preventDefault();
                return;
            }

            var frm = $(this);
            var trackEventName = frm.attr('name');
            var eventCategory = frm.find('input[name="event_category"]').val();
            $.ajax({
                url: frm.attr('action'),
                type: frm.attr('method'),
                data: frm.serialize(),
                success: function(data) {
                    var resp = JSON.parse(data);
                    switch (resp.status_code) {
                        case 1:
                            showModal('confirmation_fehler_aufgetreten', frm);
                            break;
                        case 6:
                            showModal('confirmation_bestätigung', frm);
                            break;
                        case 5:
                            showModal('confirmation_not_bestätigung', frm);
                            break;
                        case 4:
                            showModal('confirmation_erfolgreich', frm);
                            break;
                        case 7:
                            showModal('confirmation_bereits_angemeldet', frm);
                            break;
                        default:
                            break;
                    }
                    _paq.push(["trackEvent", eventCategory, "click", trackEventName]);
                }
            });
        });

        // Close modal function
        function closeModal(modalId) {
            const confirmation = document.getElementById(modalId);
            const overlay = document.getElementById('overlay');
            if(confirmation && overlay) {
                if (window.innerWidth <= 639) {
                    confirmation.style.animation = 'slideOutLoginbox 1s forwards';
                    overlay.style.animation = 'fadeOut 0.5s forwards';

                    confirmation.addEventListener('animationend', function() {
                        confirmation.style.display = 'none';
                        overlay.style.display = 'none';
                        hideNewsletterBox();
                    }, { once: true });
                } else {
                    confirmation.style.display = 'none';
                    overlay.style.display = 'none';
                    hideNewsletterBox();
                }
            }
        }

        // hide the Article newsletter sign-up box
        function hideNewsletterBox() {
            var newsletterBox = $('.hide-article-newsletter-box');
            if (newsletterBox.length) {
                newsletterBox.hide();
            }
        }

        // Show modal function
        function showModal(modalId, frm) {
            const overlay = document.getElementById('overlay');
            const confirmation = document.getElementById(modalId);
            if (confirmation && overlay) {
                confirmation.style.display = 'block';
                confirmation.style.animation = 'slideInLoginbox 1s forwards';
                overlay.style.animation = 'fadeIn 0.5s forwards';
                overlay.style.display = 'block';
                frm.find('input[type="email"]').val(''); // Clear the email input for the specific form
            }

        }
        // Attach close event to all close buttons in any modal
        document.querySelectorAll('.modal .x-svg').forEach(function(closeButton) {
            closeButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                const modal = this.closest('.modal');
                if (modal) {
                    closeModal(modal.id);
                }
            });
        });
    });

    function trackEvent(category, action, name, c_float) {
        var trackingData = ['trackEvent', category, action, name, c_float];
        _paq.push(trackingData);
        //console.log('Tracking data sent:', trackingData);
    }
</script>

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
        // console.log('Cookie: ' + parent.NW.getCookieValue('show-drive'));
        // setCookie no-drive


                    if (window.location.href == 'https://www.nw.de/' || window.location.href.includes('jdbg')) {
                checkVendorConsent('c26049', ajaxCallDriveRecos('lokales')); //'c26049' - drive vendor id
                checkVendorConsent('c26049', ajaxCallDriveRecos('top-individual')); //'c26049' - drive vendor id
            }
            }, false);
    
    function checkVendorConsent(vendorId, callback) {
        let interval = setInterval(function () {
            if (typeof getCMPData === 'undefined' || Object.keys(getCMPData.vendorConsents).length === 0) {
                clearInterval(interval);
                checkVendorConsent(vendorId, callback);
            } else {
                if (vendorId in getCMPData.vendorConsents && getCMPData.vendorConsents[vendorId]) {
                    callback && callback();
                }
                clearInterval(interval);
                return;
            }
        }, 200);
    }

        let options = {
        root: null,
        rootMargin: '0px',
        threshold: 1.0
    }
    let alreadyIntersected = [];
    let IntersectionObservercallback = (entries, observer) => {
        entries.forEach((entry) => {
            if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                let property = {
                    article_id: entry.target.getAttribute('data-article-id'),
                    correlation_id: entry.target.getAttribute('data-correlation-id'),
                    is_plus: (entry.target.getAttribute('data-is-plus') == 1),
                    plus_sign_visible: (entry.target.getAttribute('data-plus-sign-visible') == 1),
                    box_type: 'box',  // Box-Typ: slider, box oder null
                    position_in_box: parseInt(entry.target.getAttribute('data-article-position'))
                }

                if (!alreadyIntersected.includes(property.article_id)) {
                    window.drive && window.drive(
                        "trackSelfDescribingEvent",
                        {
                            schema: "iglu:de.drive/recommendation_exposure/jsonschema/1-0-0",
                            data: property,
                        },
                        [
                            {
                                schema: 'iglu:de.drive/box_context/jsonschema/1-0-0',
                                data: {
                                    box_title: entry.target.getAttribute('data-boxname'),  // Titel der Personalisierungsbox
                                    num_articles_in_box: 3,  // Anzahl Artikel in der Box
                                    box_x_start: 100.0000, // Startposition X der Box
                                    box_y_start: 100.0000, // Startposition Y der Box
                                    width: 100.0000,  // Breite in Pixel
                                    height: 100.0000, // Höhe in Pixel
                                }
                            },
                            {
                                schema: "iglu:de.drive/recommendation_retrieval_context/jsonschema/1-0-0",
                                data: {
                                    load_time_ms: 120.0 // Antwortzeit der DRIVE API
                                }
                            }
                        ]
                    );
                }
                // nur einmal Intersection als exposure an drive senden
                alreadyIntersected.push(property.article_id);
                return;
            }
        });
    };
    let observer = new IntersectionObserver(IntersectionObservercallback, options);

    function monitorDriveRecoExposure() {
        let target = document.querySelectorAll('.drive-reco');
        target.forEach((elem) => {
            observer.observe(elem);
        });
    }
    
        function addClickEventsToDriveRecos() {
        // Reco-Clicks
        var driveRecoLinks = document.getElementsByClassName('drive-reco');
        var i = driveRecoLinks.length;
        while (i--) {
            driveRecoLinks[i].addEventListener('click', driveRecoClick);
        }
    }

    function driveRecoClick() {
        let property = {
            "article_id": this.getAttribute('data-article-id'),
            "correlation_id": this.getAttribute('data-correlation-id')
        }
        // let experimentGroup = this.getAttribute('data-exp-group');

        // window.drive('trackStructEvent', 'experiment', 'click', 'owl-personalisierung-baumfalke', JSON.stringify(property), experimentGroup);
        window.drive(
            "trackSelfDescribingEvent",
            {
                schema: "iglu:de.drive/recommendation_click/jsonschema/1-0-0",
                data: property
            },
            [
                {
                    schema: 'iglu:de.drive/box_context/jsonschema/1-0-0',
                    data: {
                        box_title: this.getAttribute('data-boxname'),  // Titel der Personalisierungsbox
                        num_articles_in_box: 4,  // Anzahl Artikel in der Box
                        box_x_start: 100.0000, // Startposition X der Box
                        box_y_start: 100.0000, // Startposition Y der Box
                        width: 100.0000,  // Breite in Pixel
                        height: 100.0000, // Höhe in Pixel
                    }
                },
                {
                    schema: "iglu:de.drive/recommendation_retrieval_context/jsonschema/1-0-0",
                    data: {
                        load_time_ms: 120.0 // Antwortzeit der DRIVE API
                    }
                }
            ]
        );
    }
    
        function ajaxCallDriveRecos(id) {
        var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
        xhr.onload = function () {

            if (xhr.status >= 200 && xhr.status < 300) {
                let response = xhr.response;
                if (response.length > 200 && document.getElementById(id) !== null) {
                    document.getElementById(id).innerHTML = response;
                }

                // CMS-Teaser mit drive-Attributen bestücken
                try {
                                            if (id === 'top-individual' && document.getElementById(id) !== null) {
                                            var attributes = JSON.parse(response);
                        var i = 1;

                            if (id == 'modul_13226') {
                                // alert("Gruppe: B, Fallback: " + ((attributes['data-fallback'] === '1' ) ? 'Ja' : 'Nein'));
                                console.log(document.getElementById(id).querySelectorAll('article'));
                            }

                        document.getElementById(id).querySelectorAll('article').forEach(function (element) {
                            for (const key in attributes) {
                                element.setAttribute(`${key}`, `${attributes[key]}`);
                            }
                            element.setAttribute(`data-article-position`, i);
                            i++;
                            element.classList.add('drive-reco');
                        });
                    }
                } catch(err) {
                    // console.log(err);
                }
                // bind drive reco click event
                addClickEventsToDriveRecos();
                // monitor drive reco exposure
                monitorDriveRecoExposure();

                return response;
            } else {
                // Runs when it's not
                // console.log(xhr.responseText);
            }
        }

        xhr.open('GET', 'https://www.nw.de/_em_daten/locals/module/nw/_includes/twig/current/public/scripts/drive-ajax.php?id=' + id + '&mandant=nw' + '&' + Date.now());
        xhr.send();
                    setTimeout(function (){loadEngagentlyCounters();}, 2000);
            }
        // This function is called after your AJAX call completes
        function loadEngagentlyCounters() {
            // Find all elements that have a data-egy-dsc attribute within the newly loaded content
            engagentlyCommentCount('.customTeasers[data-egy-dsc]')
        }

</script>

<script>
    function triggerAboFooter() {

        const footer = document.getElementById('nw-paywall-footer');
        const aboFooterClosed = localStorage.getItem('abofooterClosedSommer');
        console.log('Footer :', aboFooterClosed);


        if ((aboFooterClosed === null || aboFooterClosed === "false")&&userstatus_upscore<2) {
            console.log("No-Plus"+ userstatus_upscore);
            footer.classList.remove('nw-hidden');
            _paq.push(["trackEvent", "footer-widget", "view", "Abofooter", 4738]);
        }
    }
    function toggleFooter() {
        const collapsed = document.getElementById('footerCollapsed');
        const expanded = document.getElementById('footerExpanded');
        const arrow = document.querySelector('#toggleArrow svg');
        const toggleButton = document.getElementById('toggleArrow');

        collapsed.classList.toggle('nw-hidden');
        expanded.classList.toggle('nw-hidden');

        arrow.classList.toggle('nw-rotate-180');

        const isExpanded = expanded.classList.contains('nw-hidden') === false;
        toggleButton.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isExpanded);
    }

    function closeFooter() {
        const footer = document.getElementById('nw-paywall-footer');
        if (footer) {
            localStorage.setItem('abofooterClosedSommer', 'true');
            footer.classList.add('nw-hidden');
        }
    }





</script>

                        <script type="text/javascript">
                            $(document).ready(function () {
                                var frm_footer = $('#nl-anmeldung-footer');
                                var message = '';
                                $('#referrer_url-footer').val(window.location.href);

                                frm_footer.submit(function (event) {
                                    event.preventDefault();

                                    $.ajax({
                                        url: frm_footer.attr('action'),
                                        type: "POST",
                                        data: frm_footer.serialize(),
                                        success: function (data) {
                                            var resp = JSON.parse(data);
                                            $('#nl-anmeldung-footer').hide();
                                            if (resp.success == 1) {
                                                if (resp.message == "Sie sind bereits angemeldet.") {
                                                    $('#nl-message-footer').text(resp.message);
                                                } else {
                                                    $('#nl-message-footer').show().text('Wunderbar. Fast geschafft!');
                                                }
                                                _paq.push(["trackEvent", "NL-Footer", "click", "Red_Newsletter__Mittagsnotiz"]);
                                            }
                                            message = escape(resp.message);
                                            $('#nl-selligent-message-footer').show().text(decodeURIComponent(unescape(message)));
                                            //_paq.push(['FormAnalytics::trackFormConversion', 'nl_update_zum_mittag', 'nl-anmeldung']);
                                        },
                                        error: function (data) {
                                            var resp = JSON.parse(data);
                                            $('#nl-selligent-message-footer').show().text(resp.message);
                                        }
                                    });
                                });
                            });
                        </script>
